Across Three Major Projects\\n\\nAfter analyzing kubernetes/kubernetes, grafana/grafana, and prometheus/prometheus, three distinct but related patterns emerge for how Prometheus metrics are created and registered with a metric registry.\\n\\n### Kubernetes Pattern: Wrapped Metrics with Legacy Registry\\n\\nKubernetes uses a custom abstraction layer (`k8s.io/component-base/metrics`) that wraps Prometheus client_golang. Key characteristics:\\n\\n**Metric Creation (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go, lines 134-257):**\\n- Metrics are created using wrapped constructors like `metrics.NewHistogramVec()` and `metrics.NewCounterVec()` from the k8s.io/component-base/metrics package\\n- Metrics include stability level annotations (e.g., `metrics.STABLE`, `metrics.ALPHA`, `metrics.BETA`)\\n- Metrics support namespace, subsystem, and name organization\\n\\n**Registration Pattern (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go, lines 260-268):**\\n- Uses `legacyregistry.MustRegister()` to register metrics into the global Prometheus registry\\n- Implements custom `mustRegister()` methods on metric set types (line 339)\\n- Defers registration using `sync.Once` for lazy initialization in some cases\\n- Example: The metricSet type defines `mustRegister()` method that calls `legacyregistry.MustRegister(m.latencies)` for each metric\\n\\n**Registry Management (staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/metrics/registry.go):**\\n- Provides `kubeRegistry` type with `RegisterMetaMetrics()` and `MustRegister()` methods\\n- Supports custom registries and registration with error handling\\n- Manages registration of meta-metrics about registered metrics themselves\\n\\nThis pattern is used throughout Kubernetes in files like pkg/kubelet/metrics/metrics.go, pkg/proxy/metrics/metrics.go, and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/metrics.go.\\n\\n### Grafana Pattern: Flexible Registration with promauto and Custom Registries\\n\\nGrafana uses Prometheus client_golang directly but adds flexible registration patterns. Key characteristics:\\n\\n**Metric Creation (apps/plugins/pkg/app/metrics/metrics.go, lines 14-61):**\\n- Uses direct Prometheus constructors: `prometheus.NewCounterVec()`, `prometheus.NewHistogramVec()`, `prometheus.NewHistogram()`\\n- Metrics are created as package-level variables with Prometheus defaults\\n- Supports namespace organization\\n\\n**Registration Pattern 1 - Custom MustRegister Function (apps/plugins/pkg/app/metrics/metrics.go, lines 64-82):**\\n- Implements custom `MustRegister(registerer prometheus.Registerer)` function that accepts a custom registry\\n- Iterates over metrics and calls `registerer.Register()` with error handling\\n- Gracefully handles AlreadyRegisteredError to allow safe re-registration\\n\\n**Registration Pattern 2 - PromaAuto with Custom Registries (pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/historian.go, lines 39-60):**\\n- Uses `promauto.With(r).NewCounterVec()` pattern where r is a custom prometheus.Registerer\\n- This automatically registers metrics with the provided registry during construction\\n- Reduces boilerplate by combining metric creation and registration\\n\\n**Registration Pattern 3 - Direct PromaAuto (pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/datasource_metrics_middleware.go, lines 15-36):**\\n- Uses `promauto.NewCounterVec()` to automatically register with the default Prometheus registry\\n- Simplest pattern when using global registry\\n\\n**Registration Pattern 4 - Custom Registry with MustRegister Method (pkg/infra/httpclient/httpclientprovider/prometheus_metrics_middleware.go, lines 50-62):**\\n- Implements `MustRegister(registry prometheus.Registerer)` and `WithMustRegister()` methods\\n- Allows chaining for inline initialization\\n- Provides both registration and builder patterns\\n\\nThis flexible approach is used throughout Grafana in files like pkg/services/dashboards/service/metrics.go, pkg/storage/unified/resource/metrics.go, and pkg/services/ngalert/metrics/scheduler.go.\\n\\n### Prometheus Pattern: Direct Client with Init-Based Registration\\n\\nPrometheus uses prometheus client_golang directly with initialization functions. Key characteristics:\\n\\n**Metric Creation (storage/remote/write.go, lines 38-55):**\\n- Uses `promauto.NewCounter()` and `promauto.NewCounterVec()` for automatic registration to the default registry\\n- Metrics are created as package-level variables\\n- Supports namespace and subsystem organization\\n\\n**Registration Pattern 1 - Init Functions (web/federate.go, lines 56-59, template/template.go, lines 56-59):**\\n- Uses `init()` functions that call `prometheus.MustRegister()` with metrics as arguments\\n- Simple and direct approach for global registry metrics\\n- Panics if metric already registered\\n\\n**Registration Pattern 2 - Custom Registry with Conditional Registration (rules/group.go, lines 1056-1070):**\\n- Accepts a custom `prometheus.Registerer` as a parameter\\n- Calls `reg.MustRegister()` on metrics only if registry is not nil\\n- Supports both global and custom registry patterns\\n- Metrics are created as fields in struct types (e.g., GroupMetrics struct)\\n\\n**Registration Pattern 3 - Registry in Constructor (storage/remote/write.go, lines 81-112):**\\n- Passes registry to constructor functions like `NewWriteStorage()`\\n- Creates metrics within constructor if registry is provided\\n- Calls `reg.MustRegister()` on created metrics\\n- Allows both global and custom registries\\n\\n**Registration Pattern 4 - PromaAuto (storage/remote/write.go, lines 38-55):**\\n- Uses `promauto.NewCounter()` for automatic registration without explicit registry\\n- Simplifies metric creation and registration into single step\\n\\nThis pattern is used throughout Prometheus in files like rules/group.go, tsdb/compact.go, tsdb/head.go, scrape/metrics.go, and notifier/metric.go.\\n\\n### Key Differences\\n\\n1. **Abstraction Level**: Kubernetes wraps the Prometheus client with additional features (stability levels, meta-metrics), while Grafana and Prometheus use the client more directly\\n\\n2. **Registry Flexibility**: Grafana emphasizes flexible, reusable registration functions that accept custom registries, while Prometheus prioritizes simplicity with init functions and promauto\\n\\n3. **Registration Timing**: Kubernetes often defers registration with sync.Once, Grafana typically registers in constructors, and Prometheus combines both approaches\\n\\n4. **Error Handling**: Grafana explicitly handles AlreadyRegisteredError for idempotent registration, while Kubernetes and Prometheus rely on MustRegister panicking\\n\\n5. **Metric Organization**: All three use namespace/subsystem/name, but Kubernetes adds stability level as a first-class concept\\n\\nThe three patterns represent a spectrum of abstraction and flexibility, with Kubernetes providing the most structure, Prometheus providing the most simplicity, and Grafana balancing both with maximum registry flexibility.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":6863,"cache_read_input_tokens":64450,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":6863},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"cc3d9380-1a5b-4768-b8b4-c4be513a5477","uuid":"06ba46af-facb-4449-9f7f-64ed84e5922a"}
